<Review>I love this place! I wish it was closer to me but it was worth the 30 minutes drive. I ordered online and the time slots were perfect for me. There's an estimated time for when the drinks were ready but it was faster than the estimated time. There was someone outside who helped with giving out orders and I think that was great. I was worried because the drinks were already done and I didn't pick them up for another 10+ minutes and the biggest thing about that is usually the ice. This is my favorite Boba place in the Bay Area and I've tried a lot.. great seasonal drinks and their regular drinks are always consistent and yummy. I love supporting this Asian women-owned small business run by sisters. When the pandemic hit they quickly found a way to make ordering easier online and have a great pick up system. No more waiting in line! They also take the time and effort to support frontline healthcare workers and the Asian community.</Review>

< Text>
Great new boba place that replaced tea factory. I had my reservations about it since there are so many new boba places but, from the two times I've been there, it has been very solid. I had the Jasmine milk tea the first time and it had a great Jasmine tea flavor. I thought it was a tad too milky for me but fine otherwise. The boba is also good. It has a nice chew and isn't too sweet. The next visit, I got the strawberry matcha latte and I have to say, it's at least as good as boba guys. The strawberry puree in it was great and paired well with the matcha. I'll definitely be back.

On a side note, they do have a variety of milk substitutes. They include almond and the increasingly popular, oat milk. The milk substitutes don't cost more which is very nice of them.< /Text>

<userid>111276956218589796335</userid><review>This place took over the former Saigon Bliss Pho restaurant. We were saddened because we wanted to get pho and then boba. But glad to know it runs in the same family since the Pho was owned by the mother and now the daughter owns the boba. She‚Äôs super nice and friendly when taking our order.

The menu and concept reminds me of boba shops in Orange County due to the drink flavors, serving snacks, and concept. Unlike other SD tea shops that are Taiwanese/Chinese, I am happy that we have a Vietnamese inspired shop that offers flavors like durian, penny worth, sugar cane, pandan, mung bean, etc. I also love that the menu offers picture with description and not just a list of names and you don‚Äôt know what to order.

We got Mr. Bean which was a mix of mung bean and infused with pandan leaves along with crystal boba. The texture is there but not as rich if I were to compare it to my favorite place in OC but it‚Äôs just as good because of the infused pandan which probably took away that mung bean richness but overall, two thumbs up. I‚Äôm also not a fan of boba but decided to keep it original to stick with the crystal boba. Which is way better than regular black boba since it‚Äôs like crunchy jelly not chewy starch.

We also got Jade which is Hokkaido milk tea with crystal boba and butterfly pea tea. This drink has caffeine, you can taste the strong tea and it‚Äôs legit. We got no boba for this drink.

She didn‚Äôt ask me but the person before requested their sugar level to be half sweet. So that‚Äôs a suggestion if you want to adjust your sugars and perhaps ice level. I kept it normal for my first time to see how the original tasted before any adjustments.

We ordered popcorn chicken, chicken wings, and dynamite fries. You get the most bang for your buck with pop corn chicken, it‚Äôs a large portion. The wings came with 6 so it‚Äôs like $1 a piece. I got spicy but it tasted like it wasn‚Äôt even mild. Although it was nicely breaded and meaty. The dynamite shoe string fries was yummy but the sriracha and spicy Mayo was only squirted on top and not evenly throughout underneath. So once you finish the top layer, the rest is just the saltiness and furikake. Still good but I would recommend to scatter evenly throughout. My favorite would be the pop corn chicken.

I wish there was outdoor tables for dining. Inside is available for sit down. Outside is just a white ottoman.

We came before sun down and the place started to transform from day to night as they rolled out the VIP red velvet rope and turned on the LED neon lights, club-like environment.

In my opinion, Luxe is comparable to OC boba shops and now we don‚Äôt have to drive 1.5 hours for quality drinks.</review></record>

<rating>1< /rating>< Text>
While a lot of the other reviews highly recommend this place, I cannot attest to being on the same page as them. Three years ago, I did everything I could to find a great dentist: checked reviews, looked up credentials, and even talked to former patients. Everything lead me to this establishment. However, I was stuck with a rookie dentist who messed up an expensive crown, as well as a filling. It could be my fault considering the time restraints I had put on both them and myself, but they insisted they could handle it and get everything done.
Getting the crown installed was simple, but I immediately noticed something was off. I even went back to explain my frustrations and asked what could be done, but they said "... some crowns just take time and the sensitvity should go away." It is a mistake on my behalf for believing that, considering two of the other crowns I had installed at the same time (within weeks of each other) felt absolutely great. I even expressed to the second doctor that I was handed off to, that the cement had chipped off one night while flossing and they insisted it was normal. While that may be the case in some instances, this was totally abnormal considering the entire lining of the tooth between my gum was exposed and extremely sensitive. Another thing they expressed as being normal. Three years down the road, the sensitivity has gotten so much worse that it is almost unbearable. I now have to get the crown replaced at a three year mark when they are guaranteed to be good for at least twenty. A $500 investment, after insurance I remind you, down the drain. The filling that I had done I'd also like to blame on the rookie dentist. A tooth that is mean to grind (one of the molars), she had left a gaping canyon within, as well as leaving sharp and jagged edges. During the filling, the dentist had tried to upsale me a few different times on something else, but to me a filling is a filling - and one would expect a dentist to fill and replace the tooth they drilled emtpy. I now have to have work redone on that tooth as well, considering how poor of a condition the dentist had left it in.
While two of the teeth are great and feel amazing, I would not recommend this place to a friend or family member unless you are local and have the time for multiple repeat visits to have issues resolved.< /Text>

< Review>
Of the pizza I have had in the city so far, Shakey's Pizza Parlor is easily one of the top in my list. (If only they delivered or were closer to me!) The deep dish is excellent, with a perfect crust, fresh sauce and great topping combinations. The thin crust is really tasty as well. I love the caprese salad as a perfect appetizer for one or two. They have a great selection of wines and beer. The atmosphere is casual, but classy and kind of fun. Service has been alternately really friendly and great, and bordering on rude and neglectful.
